add_namespace = rw_canada
add_namespace = rw_canada_news
add_namespace = canada_diplo
add_namespace = canada_debug

#The True North
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.1
	title = rw_canada.1.t
	desc = rw_canada.1.d
	picture = canada_intro

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.1.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				days = 2
				id = rw_canada.2
			}
			country_event = {
				days = 32
				id = rw_canada.4
			}
		}
	}
}

#2010 Liberal Party Convention
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.17
	title = rw_canada.17.t
	desc = rw_canada.17.d
	picture = 2010_liberal_convention
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Michael Ignatieff (Centrist)
		name = rw_canada.17.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_IGNATIEFF_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ignatieff_leads_liberals
		set_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Justin Trudeau (Liberal)
		name = rw_canada.17.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_TRUDEAU_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = trudeau_leads_liberals
		set_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = liberal
			popularity = 0.06
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Deadlock
		name = rw_canada.17.o3
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_JOBS_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_government = nationalist
			has_country_flag = layton_leads_ndp
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = liberal
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.218
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

#Fate of Manning
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.20
	title = rw_canada.20.t
	desc = rw_canada.20.d
	picture = manning_party
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Keep Manning
		name = rw_canada.20.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_MANNING_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = manning_leads_progcons
		add_political_power = 30
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_to_variable = {
		   var = CAN_quebec_tension
		   value = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Resign
		name = rw_canada.20.o2
		trigger = {
			date < 2011.3.3
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_TRUMP_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_HARPER_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_JOBS_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.21
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

#Conservative Party Convention
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.21
	title = {
		text = rw_canada.21.t_harper
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_pcs_reform }
	}
	title = {
		text = rw_canada.21.t_trump
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_pcs_progcon }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.21.d_harper
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_pcs_reform }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.21.d_trump
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_pcs_progcon }
	}
	picture = conservative_leadership_election
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_2011_elections_held }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN_preston_manning = {
				clr_character_flag = CAN_progressive_conservative_leader
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Trump
		name = rw_canada.21.o1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_pcs_progcon
		}
		set_country_flag = trump_leads_progcons
		set_country_flag = pcs_are_natcon
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_conservative
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		CAN_donald_trump = {
			promote_character = fiscal_conservative
			set_character_flag = CAN_progressive_conservative_leader
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.74
				days = 10
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_canada_news.9
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
		   var = CAN_alberta_tension
		   value = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Harper
		name = rw_canada.21.o1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_pcs_reform
		}
		set_country_flag = harper_leads_progcons
		set_country_flag = pcs_are_nationalist
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = nationalist
		}
		add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = national_conservative }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = nationalist
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_nationalist_pop = party_popularity@nationalist
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_natcon_pop = party_popularity@national_conservative
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = current_natcon_pop
					value = current_nationalist_pop
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = nationalist
					popularity = current_natcon_pop
				}	
			}
		}
		CAN_stephen_harper = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					expire = "1.1.1.1"
					desc="POLITICS_CAN_STEPHEN_HARPER_DESC"
					ideology = progressive_conservative
				}
			}
			promote_character = progressive_conservative
			set_character_flag = CAN_progressive_conservative_leader
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.08
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_conservative
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.75
				days = 10
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_canada_news.9
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
		   var = CAN_quebec_tension
		   value = 1
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = CAN_true_blue_pcs_party
			long_name  = CAN_true_blue_pcs_party_long
			ideology = nationalist
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_blue_tories_in_power
	}
}

#2011 Election
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.22
	title = rw_canada.22.t
	desc = rw_canada.22.d
	picture = can_election
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_socialist_ndp_party
				long_name = CAN_socialist_ndp_party_long
				ideology = moderate_socialist
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party
				long_name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party_long
				ideology = new_democrat
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_liberal_liberal_party
				long_name = CAN_liberal_liberal_party_long
				ideology = liberal
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_centrist_liberal_party
				long_name = CAN_centrist_liberal_party_long
				ideology = centrist
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_united_reform_pc_party_postel
				long_name = CAN_united_reform_pc_party_postel_long
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.205
				days = 365
				random_days = 40
			}
		}
	}
			
	
	option = { #Liberals
		name = rw_canada.22.o1
		ai_chance = {	
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_IGNATIEFF_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_TRUDEAU_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_ai_behavior
						option = CAN_JOBS_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = trump_leads_progcons }
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.31
				days = 2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = harper_leads_progcons }
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.33
				days = 2
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.32
				days = 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = liberal_victory
		set_country_flag = CAN_2011_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = trudeau_leads_liberals }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberal
			}
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					news_event = {
						hours = 4
						id = rw_canada_news.5
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = canada_sic_stephane_dion
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ignatieff_leads_liberals }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
			}
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					news_event = {
						hours = 4
						id = rw_canada_news.4
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = canada_sic_michael_bloomberg 
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = jobs_leads_liberals }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.1

#Layton Resignation?
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.67
	title = rw_canada.67.t
	desc = rw_canada.67.d
	picture = layton_cancer_worsens
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Resign
		name = rw_canada.67.o1
		ai_chance = {	
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_MULCAIR_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_CULLEN_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_TOPP_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_LAXER_WIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_WATKINS_WIN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_layton_resigns
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = rw_canada.68 days = 3 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
							option = CAN_MULCAIR_WIN
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
							option = CAN_CULLEN_WIN
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
							option = CAN_TOPP_WIN
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
							option = CAN_LAXER_WIN
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
							option = CAN_WATKINS_WIN
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.70 #Layton Succumbs
					days = 44
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = CAN_protect_healthcare }
					random_list = {
						seed = random
						30 = { 
							country_event = {
								id = rw_canada.70 #Layton Succumbs
								days = 44
							}
						}
						70 = { 
							country_event = {
								id = rw_canada.69 #Layton Recovers
								days = 44
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						seed = random
						50 = { 
							country_event = {
								id = rw_canada.69 #Layton Recovers
								days = 44
							}
						}

							country_event = {
								id = rw_canada.70 #Layton Succumbs
								days = 44
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Fight Cancer
		name = rw_canada.67.o2
		ai_chance = {	
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_LAYTON_SURVIVES
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_layton_cancer 
						option = CAN_LAYTON_SURVIVES
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.69 #Layton Recovers
					days = 44
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = CAN_protect_healthcare }
					random_list = {
						seed = random
						40 = { 
							country_event = {
								id = rw_canada.70 #Layton Succumbs
								days = 44
							}
						}
						60 = { 
							country_event = {
								id = rw_canada.69 #Layton Recovers
								days = 44
							}
						}
					}
				}

		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_ignatieff_tsarist_larp
		}
		CAN_michael_ignatieff = {
			set_nationality = RUS
			set_character_name = "Mikhail Ignatiev"
			set_portraits = {
				civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Michael_Ignatieff_Tsar.png" }
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					expire = "1.1.1.1"
					ideology = regency_monarchist
				}
			}
			promote_character = regency_monarchist
		}
		CAN_michael_bloomberg = {
			promote_character = centrist_ideology
		}
		RUS = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = monarchist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = monarchist
				popularity = 0.2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = "Ignatiev Court"
				long_name = "Ignatiev Court"
				ideology = monarchist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_IGN
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.97.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Bob Rae" ruling_only = yes }
		}
	}
	picture = ignatieff_resigns
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.97.o1
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Bob Rae" ruling_only = yes } }
			set_country_flag = liberal_justin_trudeau_2015
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist }
				clr_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist
				set_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				CAN_justin_trudeau = {
					promote_character = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.197
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

#Fate of the Monarchy
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.100
	title = rw_canada.100.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.100.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = royal_family_executed } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.100.d_royals_executed
		trigger = { has_global_flag = royal_family_executed }
	}
	picture = monarchy_fate
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Retain the Monarchy
		name = rw_canada.100.o1
		add_political_power = 20
		add_stability = -0.02
		set_country_flag = CAN_monarchy_kept
		add_ideas = CAN_resistance_to_the_monarchy
	}
	
	option = { #Abolish the Monarchy
		name = rw_canada.100.o2
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = 20
		set_country_flag = CAN_monarchy_abolished
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_period_of_transition
		add_ideas = CAN_legal_chaos
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_canada_news.39
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Britain Returns
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.114
	title = rw_canada.114.t
	desc = rw_canada.114.d
	picture = queen_meets_prime_minister

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		ENG = {
			is_in_faction_with = CAN
			is_subject_of = CAN
			OR = {
				has_government = national_conservative
				has_government = centrist
				has_government = liberal
				has_government = new_democrat
				has_government = nationalist
				has_government = moderate_socialist
				has_government = fascist
			}
		}
		has_completed_focus = CAN_reclaim_the_birthright
		has_idea = CAN_elizabeth_in_exile
	}

	option = { #Interesting
		name = rw_canada.114.o1
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_elizabeth_in_exile }
			remove_ideas = CAN_elizabeth_in_exile
			ENG = {
				country_event = rw_canada.115
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_king_in_exile_andrew }
			remove_ideas = CAN_king_in_exile_andrew
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CAN_king_in_exile_edward }
			remove_ideas = CAN_king_in_exile_edward
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

#I fucking LOVE OIL
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.170
	title = {
		text = rw_canada.170.t
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Rafael Edward Cruz" ruling_only = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = rw_canada.170.t_cruz
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Rafael Edward Cruz" ruling_only = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = rw_canada.170.d
	picture = big_oil_backing
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.170.o1
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
}

#F-35 debacle
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.175
	title = rw_canada.175.t
	desc = rw_canada.175.d
	picture = f35_procurement
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.175.o1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = moderate_socialist
				has_government = new_democrat
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist
					has_government = centrist
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_defense_white_paper
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.175.o2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = centrist
				has_government = liberal
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist }
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_cheaper_airplane
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.175.o3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = fascist
				has_government = national_conservative
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}
		add_ideas = CAN_hornet_replacement
	}
}

#Quebec and Alberta Rebel
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.184
	title = rw_canada.184.t
	desc = rw_canada.184.d
	picture = cascadian_rebels_forest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.184.o1
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CAN_separatist_crisis
			add_idea = CAN_separatist_crisis_worse
		}
		release = QUE
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_provinces = 1 }
		QUE = { 
			declare_war_on = { target = CAN type = annex_everything }
			QUE_pauline_marois = {
				promote_character = new_democrat_ideology
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Rebel Forces"
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}	
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Rebel Forces\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					owner = QUE
					count = 3
				}
			}
		}
		release = ALT
		subtract_from_variable = { CAN_provinces = 1 }
		ALT = {
			declare_war_on = { target = CAN type = annex_everything }
			division_template = {
				name = "Rebel Forces"
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}	
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Rebel Forces\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					owner = ALT
					count = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Trudeau Speech
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.185
	title = rw_canada.185.t
	desc = rw_canada.185.d
	picture = trudeau_new_order_speech
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Justin Trudeau"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = CAN_trudeau_commonwealth_war
		NEA = {
			exists = no 
		}
		owns_state = 360
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.185.o1
		add_ideas = CAN_commonwealth_resistance
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_bolshevik
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_bolshevik
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = CAN_nazbol_liberal_party
			long_name = CAN_nazbol_liberal_party_long
			ideology = national_bolshevik
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_trudeau_in_control
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		CAN_justin_trudeau = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					expire = "1.1.1.1"
					desc="POLITICS_CAN_JUSTIN_TRUDEAU_DESC"
					ideology = revolutionary_junta
					traits = { CAN_trudeaumania }
				}
			}
			promote_character = revolutionary_junta
		}
	}
}

#Trudeau Resigns
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.194
	title = rw_canada.194.t
	desc = rw_canada.194.d
	picture = its_trudover
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.194.o1
		retire_character = CAN_justin_trudeau
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = liberal
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { date < 2016.1.1 }
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.200
					days = 30
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.300
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_elections_in_one_month
	}
}

#Hillier Resigns
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.196
	title = rw_canada.196.t
	desc = rw_canada.196.d
	picture = hillier_resigns
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Rick J. Hillier"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = CAN_hillier_took_over
		NEA = {
			OR = {
				exists = no 
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		360 = {
			is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_canada.196.o1
		meta_effect = {
            text = {
				CAN_rick_j._hillier = {
					remove_country_leader_role = {
						ideology = [CURRENT_IDEOLOGY]
					}
				}
            }
            CURRENT_IDEOLOGY = "[ROOT.get_subideology]"
        }
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_soc_ndp_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_socialist_ndp_party
				long_name = CAN_socialist_ndp_party_long
				ideology = moderate_socialist
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_nd_ndp_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party
				long_name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party_long
				ideology = new_democrat
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_liberal_lib_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_liberal_liberal_party
				long_name = CAN_liberal_liberal_party_long
				ideology = liberal
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_centrist_lib_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_centrist_liberal_party
				long_name = CAN_centrist_liberal_party_long
				ideology = centrist
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_centrist_ndp_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party
				long_name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party_long
				ideology = centrist
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pc_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_national_conservative_party
				long_name = CAN_national_conservative_party_long
				ideology = national_conservative
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_alliance_nat_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_canadian_alliance_party
				long_name = CAN_canadian_alliance_party_long
				ideology = nationalist
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_pc_nat_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_united_reform_pc_party_postel
				long_name = CAN_united_reform_pc_party_postel_long
				ideology = nationalist
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_alliance_party_name_restore }
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_canadian_alliance_party
				long_name = CAN_canadian_alliance_party_long
				ideology = nationalist
			}
		}
	}
}

### 2015 Elections Stuff ###

#Liberal Primarty
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.197
	title = rw_canada.197.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.197.d_resigns
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2011
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_canada.197.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2011 }
		}
	}
	picture = liberal_party_convention

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {	
		has_country_flag = liberals_exist
	}

	option = { #Current Leader
		name = rw_canada.197.o1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = centrist
				has_government = liberal
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2011 }
		}
		set_country_flag = current_liberal_leader_2015
	}

	option = { #Justin Trudeau
		name = rw_canada.197.o2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = centrist
					has_government = liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2011
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Justin Trudeau" ruling_only = yes }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = liberal_justin_trudeau_2015
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist }
			clr_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist
			set_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_liberals_become_liberal_tt
		}
		CAN_justin_trudeau = {
			promote_character = social_liberal
		}
	}

	option = { #Chrystia Freeland
		name = rw_canada.197.o3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = centrist
					has_government = liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2011
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = liberal_chrystia_freeland_2015
		CAN_chrystia_freeland = {
			promote_character = social_liberal
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist }
			clr_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist
			set_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_liberals_become_liberal_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Paul Martin
		name = rw_canada.197.o4
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = centrist
					has_government = liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2011
			}
			has_completed_focus = CAN_legacy_of_martin
		}
		set_country_flag = liberal_paul_martin_2015
		CAN_paul_martin = {
			promote_character = centrist_ideology
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal }
			clr_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal

				has_government = moderate_socialist

					has_government = centrist

				}
				has_government = new_democrat
			}

		set_country_flag = current_ndp_leader_2015

			}

	}

			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = nationalist

			promote_character = progressive_conservative

	}

#2015 Election
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.200
	title = rw_canada.200.t
	desc = rw_canada.200.d
	picture = can_election
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = national_bolshevik
				has_government = revolutionary_socialist
				has_government = communist
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Donald Trump" ruling_only = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = CAN_trump_the_populist
					}
					CAN_donald_trump = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Donald_Trump_Second_Term_Angry.png" }
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = CAN_trump_the_reformer
					}
					CAN_donald_trump = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Donald_Trump_Second_Term_Happy.png" }
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					CAN_donald_trump = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Donald_Trump_Second_Term.png" }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Preston Manning" ruling_only = yes } }
				CAN_preston_manning = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Preston_Manning_2015.png" }
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Stephen Harper" ruling_only = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = { has_government = nationalist }
					CAN_stephen_harper = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Stephen_Harper_2015.png" }
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					CAN_stephen_harper = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Stephen_Harper_ProgCon_2015.png" }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Justin Trudeau" ruling_only = yes } }
				CAN_justin_trudeau = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Justin_Trudeau_2015.png" }
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Jack Layton" ruling_only = yes } }
				CAN_jack_layton = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Jack_Layton_2015.png" }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
				
	
	option = { #Liberals
		name = rw_canada.200.o1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = liberals_exist
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = CAN_alberta_tension
			value = 1
		}
		set_country_flag =  liberal_victory_2015
		set_country_flag = CAN_2015_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = liberal
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberal
			}
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
			}
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.298
				days = 12
				random_days = 34
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.299
				days = 22
				random_days = 24
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = canadian_alliance_is_relevant }
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.296
					days = 33
					random_days = 14
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = liberal_chrystia_freeland_2015
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_canada_news.14
				}
			}

			}
		}
		else_if = {

			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = liberal_paul_martin_2015
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {

					has_government = new_democrat 
					#has_country_flag = current_ndp_leader_2015
				}
				CAN_nathan_cullen = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1.1.1.1"
							ideology = democratic_socialist
						}
					}
					promote_character = democratic_socialist
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = { name = "Brian Topp" ruling_only = yes } 
					has_government = new_democrat 
					#has_country_flag = current_ndp_leader_2015
				}
				CAN_brian_topp = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1.1.1.1"
							ideology = democratic_socialist
						}
					}
					promote_character = democratic_socialist
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = { name = "Kiefer Sutherland" ruling_only = yes } 
					has_government = new_democrat 
					#has_country_flag = current_ndp_leader_2015
				}
				CAN_kiefer_sutherland = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1.1.1.1"
							ideology = democratic_socialist
						}
					}
					promote_character = democratic_socialist
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_2015_elections_held
		set_country_flag = bloc_quebecois_victory_2015
		set_party_name = {
			name = CAN_bloc_quebecois_party_long
			long_name = CAN_bloc_quebecois_party_long
			ideology = new_democrat
		}
		CAN_gilles_duceppe = {
			promote_character = quebec_nationalism
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = new_democrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.202
				days = 4
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_canada_news.330
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = CAN_alberta_tension
			value = 2
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_bloc_government
	}
	
	option = { #Trump

			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Donald Trump"
				ruling_only = yes
			}

country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.298
	title = rw_canada.298.t
	desc = rw_canada.298.d
	picture = ndp_convention

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {	
		has_country_flag = ndp_exists
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_elections_dont_happen_anymore }
	}

	option = { #Current Leader
		name = rw_canada.298.o1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = moderate_socialist
				AND = {
					has_government = centrist
					has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist
				}
				has_government = new_democrat
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = current_ndp_leader_2019
	}

	option = { #Nathan Cullen
		name = rw_canada.298.o2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ndp_leader_resigns_2015
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_government = moderate_socialist
						AND = {
							has_government = centrist
							has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist
						}
						has_government = new_democrat
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ndp_nathan_cullen_2019
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_modsoc }
			CAN_nathan_cullen = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1.1.1.1"
						ideology = democratic_socialist
					}
				}
				promote_character = democratic_socialist
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAN_nathan_cullen = {
				promote_character = new_democrat_ideology
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Jagmeet Singh

#2019 Election
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.300
	title = rw_canada.300.t
	desc = rw_canada.300.d
	picture = can_election
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = national_bolshevik
				has_government = revolutionary_socialist
				has_government = communist
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_elections_dont_happen_anymore }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_2015_elections_held } }
				set_country_flag = CAN_2015_elections_held
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Justin Trudeau" ruling_only = yes } }
				CAN_justin_trudeau = {
					set_portraits = {
						civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Justin_Trudeau_Beard.png" }
					}
				}
			}
			
			CAN_rafael_edward_cruz = {
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Ralph_Cruz_Beard.png" }
				}
			}
			
			CAN_michael_bloomberg = {
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Michael_Bloomberg_Coat.png" }
				}
			}
			
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.304
				days = 1460
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CAN_bq_stand_down }
				set_party_name = {
					name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party
					long_name = CAN_moderate_ndp_party_long
					ideology = new_democrat
				}
				retire_character = CAN_gilles_duceppe
				retire_character = CAN_yves_francois_blanchet
				retire_character = CAN_mario_beaulieu
				retire_character = CAN_martine_ouellet
			}
		}
	}
				
	
	option = { #Liberals
		name = rw_canada.300.o1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = liberals_exist
		}
		set_country_flag =  liberal_victory_2019
		set_country_flag = CAN_2019_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = liberal
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberal
			}
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
			}
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.301
				days = 12
				random_days = 34
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_chose_rustad }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.303
					days = 22
					random_days = 24
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.217
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			canada_sic_christina_freeland
			canada_fom_stephanie_dion
			canada_ind_maryann_mihychuk
			canada_nsm_dominic_leblanc
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_bloc_government
	}
	
	option = { #NDP
		name = rw_canada.300.o2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ndp_exists
		}
		set_country_flag =  ndp_victory_2019
		set_country_flag = CAN_2019_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_modsoc }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = moderate_socialist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = moderate_socialist
			}
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
			}
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = new_democrat
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = new_democrat
			}
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.302
				days = 12
				random_days = 34
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_chose_rustad }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.303
					days = 22
					random_days = 24
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = rw_canada.217
					days = 22
					random_days = 24
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			canada_sic_jagmeet_singh
			canada_fom_paul_dewar
			canada_ind_nathen_cullen
			canada_nsm_joe_comartin
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_bloc_government
	}
	
	option = { #ProgCons
		name = rw_canada.300.o3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = progcons_exist
		}
		set_country_flag =  pc_victory_2019
		set_country_flag = CAN_2019_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = pcs_are_nationalist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = nationalist
			}
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_ideas = canada_sic_andrew_scheer
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_conservative
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_conservative
			}
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_ideas = canada_sic_brad_trost
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.301
				days = 12
				random_days = 34
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.302
				days = 22
				random_days = 24
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			canada_fom_john_baird
			canada_ind_tony_clement
			canada_nsm_erin_otoole
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_bloc_government
	}

	option = { #Bloc
		name = rw_canada.300.o4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = canadian_bloc_exists
		}
		set_country_flag =  bloc_victory_2019
		set_country_flag = CAN_2019_elections_held
		add_popularity = {

		}

		hidden_effect = {

			}

				days = 12
				random_days = 34
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.303
				days = 22
				random_days = 24
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Canadian Alliance
		name = rw_canada.300.o5
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = canadian_alliance_is_relevant
		}
		set_country_flag = alliance_victory_2019

			}
		}

#Liberal Primarty
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.301
	title = rw_canada.301.t
	desc = rw_canada.301.d
	picture = liberal_party_convention

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {	
		has_country_flag = liberals_exist
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_elections_dont_happen_anymore }
	}
	
	option = { #Current Leader
		name = rw_canada.301.o1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = centrist
				has_government = liberal
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = current_liberal_leader_2023
	}

	option = { #Dominic LeBlanc
		name = rw_canada.301.o2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = centrist
					has_government = liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2015
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = liberal_dominic_leblanc_2023
		CAN_dominic_leblanc = {
			promote_character = social_liberal
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist }
			clr_country_flag = liberals_are_centrist
			set_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal
			custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_liberals_become_liberal_tt
		}
	}

	option = { #Mark Carney
		name = rw_canada.301.o3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = centrist
					has_government = liberal
				}
				has_country_flag = liberal_leader_resigns_2015

			}

#Later Election
country_event = {
	id = rw_canada.304
	title = rw_canada.304.t
	desc = rw_canada.304.d
	picture = can_election
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = national_bolshevik
				has_government = revolutionary_socialist
				has_government = communist
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_elections_dont_happen_anymore }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_canada.304
				days = 1460
			}
		}
		CAN_pierre_poilievre = {
			set_portraits = {
				civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Pierre_Poilievre_No_Glasses.png" }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = nationalist }
			CAN_donald_trump = {
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Donald_Trump_Third_Term.png" }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			CAN_donald_trump = {
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/CAN/Portrait_CAN_Donald_Trump_Third_Term_Angry.png" }
				}
			}
		}
	}
			
	
	option = { #Liberals
		name = rw_canada.304.o1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = liberals_exist
		}
		set_country_flag =  liberal_victory_2023
		set_country_flag = CAN_2023_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = liberals_are_liberal }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = liberal
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = liberal
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #NDP
		name = rw_canada.304.o2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ndp_exists
		}
		set_country_flag =  ndp_victory_2023
		set_country_flag = CAN_2023_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_modsoc }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = moderate_socialist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = moderate_socialist
			}
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
			}
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = new_democrat
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = new_democrat
			}
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #ProgCons
		name = rw_canada.304.o3
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = progcons_exist
		}
		set_country_flag =  pc_victory_2023
		set_country_flag = CAN_2023_elections_held
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = pcs_are_nationalist }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = nationalist
			}
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_conservative
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_conservative
			}
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Canadian Bloc
		name = rw_canada.304.o4
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = canadian_bloc_exists
		}
		set_country_flag =  bloc_victory_2023
		set_country_flag = CAN_2023_elections_held
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = new_democrat
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = bloc_ndp_alliance }
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}

			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes

		}
	}
	
	option = { #Canadian Alliance

			has_country_flag = canadian_alliance_is_relevant
		}
		set_country_flag = alliance_victory_2023

			}

		}
	}
	
	option = { #Green Party
		name = rw_canada.300.o6
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = green_party_is_a_thing
		}
		add_popularity = {

				days = 12

			}

				days = 12
				random_days = 34
			}

				id = rw_canada.303
				days = 22
				random_days = 24
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = CAN_bloc_government
		set_country_flag = CAN_green_party
		add_ideas = {
			canada_sic_annamie_paul
			canada_fom_paul_manly

#Northwest Conqured
country_event = {
	id = canada_diplo.25
	title = canada_diplo.25.t
	desc = canada_diplo.25.d
	picture = northwest_falls

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		388 = { 
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					NOT = { has_government = fascist }
				}
			}
		}
		387 = { 
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					NOT = { has_government = fascist }
				}
			}
		}
		LIN = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		MOT = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_intervention_in_the_northwest
			has_completed_focus = CAN_no_more_ethnostates
		}
		NOT = {
			387 = { 
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = PCA
						tag = MWA
						tag = AMC
						tag = LIN
						tag = USA
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			388 = { 
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = PCA
						tag = MWA
						tag = AMC
						tag = LIN
						tag = USA
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_became_usa }
	}
	
	option = { #Good
		name = canada_diplo.25.o1
		release = LIN
		release = MOT
		if = {
			limit = {
				LIN = { is_subject_of = CAN }
			}
			end_puppet = LIN
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MOT = { is_subject_of = CAN }
			}
			end_puppet = MOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				MOT = {
					owns_state = 387
				}
			}
			MOT = {
				release = LIN
			}
			CAN = {
				puppet = LIN
			}
		}
		MOT = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = nationalist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist 
				popularity = 0.25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_canadian_occupation_party
				long_name = CAN_canadian_occupation_party_long
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MOT_CAN
			add_ideas = CAN_canadian_mission_idea
		}
		LIN = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = nationalist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist 
				popularity = 0.25
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_canadian_occupation_party
				long_name = CAN_canadian_occupation_party_long
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = LIN_CAN
			add_ideas = CAN_canadian_mission_idea
		}
		CAN_david_fraser = {
			set_nationality = MOT
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = { ideology = military_junta }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
		}
		CAN_ray_henault = {
			set_nationality = LIN
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = { ideology = military_junta }
				promote_leader = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#Fate of America
country_event = {
	id = canada_diplo.32
	title = canada_diplo.32.t
	desc = canada_diplo.32.d
	picture = canada_us_relations

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		#has_completed_focus = CAN_a_disunited_america
		MWA = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		GRL = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		MOT = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		LIN = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		PCA = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		TEX = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		UTA = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		ARI = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
		}
		CAN_america_is_controlled = yes
	}
	
	option = { #Absorb America
		name = canada_diplo.32.o1
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_post_america_nation = yes 
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
			CAN = {
				annex_country = { 
					target = PREV 
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		enable_unification_decisions = yes
		core_NEA = yes
		core_ILL = yes
		core_GRL = yes
		core_MWA = yes
		core_MOT = yes
		core_LIN = yes
		core_UTA = yes
		core_ARI = yes
		core_PCA = yes
		core_TEX = yes
		core_USA = yes
		set_country_flag = CAN_became_usa
	}
	
	option = { #Form United America
		name = canada_diplo.32.o2
		create_dynamic_country = {	#United America
			original_tag = MWA
			copy_tag = MWA
			
			transfer_state = 382
			add_state_core = 382
			
			save_global_event_target_as = united_american_puppet

			### Politics
			set_popularities = {
				fascist = 0
				nationalist = 10
				monarchist = 0
				national_bolshevik = 0
				national_conservative = 20
				centrist = 20
				liberal = 20
				new_democrat = 20
				moderate_socialist = 10
				revolutionary_socialist = 0
				communist = 0
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = centrist
				long_name = "United America"
				name = "United America"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = nationalist
				long_name = "United America"
				name = "United America"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_conservative
				long_name = "United America"
				name = "United America"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = liberal
				long_name = "United America"
				name = "United America"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = moderate_socialist
				long_name = "United America"
				name = "United America"
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = AMR_CONFED
		}
		event_target:united_american_puppet = { 
			get_current_government_type = yes
		}
		CAN = {
			puppet = event_target:united_american_puppet
		}
		event_target:united_american_puppet = { 
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
		AMR_council_of_america = {
			set_nationality = event_target:united_american_puppet
		}
		event_target:united_american_puppet = { 
			AMR_council_of_america = {
				promote_character = centrist_ideology
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader={
						ideology=nationalist_ideology
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						id=-1
					}
					country_leader={
						ideology=reactionary
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						id=-1
					}
					country_leader={
						ideology=social_liberal
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						id=-1
					}
					country_leader={
						ideology=new_democrat_ideology
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						id=-1
					}
					country_leader={
						ideology=moderate_socialist_ideology
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						id=-1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_us_state = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = CAN }
			}
			event_target:united_american_puppet = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_post_america_nation = yes 
				is_subject_of = CAN
			}
			event_target:united_american_puppet = { 
				annex_country = { 
					target = PREV 
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_american_mainland_state = yes }
			event_target:united_american_puppet = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			news_event = rw_canada_news.12
		}
	}
	option = { #Nothing
		name = canada_diplo.32.o3
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

		name = canada_diplo.42.o1
	    ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		CAN = {
		    country_event = { days = 1 id = canada_diplo.43 } 
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		
	}
	
	option = { #No
		name = canada_diplo.42.o2
	    ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 40
				AND = { #Countries are less likely to join if they are just Commonwealth members
					has_idea = idea_eng_commonwealth_member
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_government = national_conservative
							has_government = centrist
							has_government = liberal
							has_government = new_democrat
							has_government = moderate_socialist
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		CAN = {
		    country_event = { days = 1 id = canada_diplo.44 } 
		}
	}
}

#Jean speaks up
country_event = {
	id = canada_diplo.59
	title = canada_diplo.59.t
	desc = canada_diplo.59.d
	picture = jean_speaks_up
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_character = {
				limit = {
					is_army_leader = yes
					NOT = {
						is_character = CAN_rick_j._hillier
						is_character = CAN_ray_henault
						is_character = CAN_david_fraser
					}
				}
				set_variable = { CAN.CAN_haiti_expedition_leader = THIS }
				set_character_flag = CAN_haiti_expedition_leader
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Can't someone else deal with this mess?
		name = canada_diplo.59.o1
	    add_stability = -0.03
		CAN_subtract_3_percent_popularity = yes
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	
	option = { #Fine, we'll do something
		name = canada_diplo.59.o2
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = 0.02
		random_character = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = CAN_haiti_expedition_leader }
			set_nationality = HAI
		}
		HAI = {
			random_character = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = CAN_haiti_expedition_leader }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = { ideology = centrist_ideology }
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = CAN_multinational_mission_party
				long_name = CAN_multinational_mission_party_long
				ideology = centrist
			}
		}
		news_event = {
			id = canada_diplo.60
			hours = 4
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = CAN_haiti_mission
			set_country_flag = CAN_intervened_in_haiti
			HAI = { 
				get_current_government_type = yes
			}
			CAN = { puppet = HAI }
			HAI = { 
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
		}

			USA = { exists = yes has_idea = idea_standing_firm_remnants }
		}
	}
}

	}

		name = can_separatism.3.o2
		add_political_power = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {	
				limit = {
					check_variable = {

					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = can_separatism.4
						days = 70

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = can_separatism.26
	title = can_separatism.25.t
	desc = can_separatism.25.d
	picture = alberta_votes_leave

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = can_separatism.25.o1
		CAN_subtract_5_percent_popularity = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			release = ALT
			subtract_from_variable = { CAN_provinces = 1 }
			ALT = { 
				get_current_government_type = yes
			}

#Attacks Intensify
country_event = {
	id = can_separatism.32
	title = can_separatism.32.t
	desc = {
		text = can_separatism.32.d_quebec
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_in_crisis }
	}
	desc = {
		text = can_separatism.32.d_alberta
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CAN_alberta_in_crisis }
	}
	desc = {
		text = can_separatism.32.d_both
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = CAN_alberta_in_crisis 
			has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_in_crisis 
		}
	}
	picture = miami_communist_attack

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = CAN_alberta_in_crisis_idea
			has_idea = CAN_quebec_in_crisis_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_alberta_in_crisis
			}
			MOT = { is_subject = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CAN_quebec_in_crisis
			}
			NEA = { has_government = revolutionary_socialist }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = can_separatism.32.o1
		random_owned_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.06
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.06
			}
		}
		add_manpower = -400
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = NEA_is_afraid_of_canada } }
				country_event = {
					id = can_separatism.33
					days = 47
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = can_separatism.37
	title = can_separatism.37.t
	desc = can_separatism.37.d
	picture = hillier_takes_over

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = can_separatism.37.o1
		set_country_flag = CAN_hillier_took_over
		meta_effect = {
            text = {
				CAN_rick_j._hillier = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1.1.1.1"
							ideology = [CURRENT_IDEOLOGY]
						}
					}
					promote_character = [CURRENT_IDEOLOGY]
				}
            }
            CURRENT_IDEOLOGY = "[ROOT.get_subideology]"
        }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = moderate_socialist
			}
			set_party_name = {
				long_name = CAN_unity_party_long
				name = CAN_unity_party
				ideology = moderate_socialist
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_soc_ndp_party_name_restore
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = new_democrat
			}
			set_party_name = {
				long_name = CAN_unity_party_long
				name = CAN_unity_party
				ideology = new_democrat
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_nd_ndp_party_name_restore
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = liberal
				has_country_flag = ndp_is_liberal
			}
			set_party_name = {
				long_name = CAN_unity_party_long
				name = CAN_unity_party
				ideology = liberal
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_liberal_ndp_party_name_restore
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = liberal
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_liberal }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				long_name = CAN_unity_party_long
				name = CAN_unity_party
				ideology = liberal
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_liberal_lib_party_name_restore
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = centrist
				has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist
			}
			set_party_name = {
				long_name = CAN_unity_party_long
				name = CAN_unity_party
				ideology = centrist
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_centrist_ndp_party_name_restore
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = centrist
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ndp_is_centrist }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				long_name = CAN_unity_party_long
				name = CAN_unity_party
				ideology = centrist
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_centrist_lib_party_name_restore
			add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
			add_modsoc_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		else_if = {

			}

			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes

				ideology = nationalist
			}

			}

#2010 Stanley Cup 
country_event = {
	id = can_flavour.3
	title = can_flavour.3.t
	desc = can_flavour.3.d
	picture = 2010_stanley_cup

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			tag = CAN
			tag = ARI
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_global_flag = CAN_senators_win_cup
		clr_global_flag = ARI_coyotes_win_cup
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				45 = { #Ottawa wins
					set_global_flag = CAN_senators_win_cup
				}
				55 = { #Arizona wins
					set_global_flag = ARI_coyotes_win_cup
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = can_flavour.3.o1
		trigger = { tag = CAN }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = can_flavour.5 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = can_flavour.4 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = can_flavour.o2.b
		trigger = { tag = ARI }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = can_flavour.5 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = can_flavour.4 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}
